 pradhanmantri narendra modi ne biplab deb ko unke vivaadaaspad bayanon ke liye talab kiya he
 According to party sources, Biplab Debco has been asked to come to Delhi
 deb ko piem modi or bijepi adhyaksh amit shah se rashtriya rajdhani main do may ko mulaakaat karne ke liye kaha gaya he
 According to sources, senior party leaders are upset with the controversy arising out of Deb's statements
 deb kuch bhi bolte ja rahe hai, modi unase baat karenge
 Let me tell you that Deb has not even taken two months to take oath as the Chief Minister of Tripura and he has given many such statements, which have been widely criticized
 haal hi main vah civil sarvice kii taiyaari kar rahe chaatro ko ajeebogareeb salaah dekar charchaa main rahe
 Deb said that only civil engineers should apply for the civil service examination
 iske peeche unka tark bhi hairaan karne vaala he
 He says that one should not go into civil services after doing mechanical engineering
 biplab deb kaa yah bayaan civil sarvice pariksha kaa rigelt aane ke baad aayaa
 Earlier in the Mahabharata period, Biplab Deb has also made controversial statements about Indian beauty in Internet and Miss World
 unhone nai scientific theory dete hue daawa kiya tha ki internet mahabharat ke daur main bhi tha or tab iskaa istemaal kiya jaataa tha
 He also claimed that satellites were also present in that era
 biplab kumaar debane dyna heden ko 1997 main miss world kaa khitaab die jane par bhi sawaal uthaa chuke hai
 He had said that Diana Hayden's victory was a fix
 vahiin, unhone aishwarya raay kii tarif karte hue kaha tha ki sahi myne main aishwarya bhartiya mahilaon kii numaaindgi karti hai
 There is no proposal from the Central Government to enact a law to prevent incidents of conversion from time to time in the country
 grih rajyamantri ajay maakan ne aaj loksabhaa main prahlada joshi ke prashn ke likhit uttar main kaha ki kuch sasthanon ke dharmaataran main kathith taur par sanlipt paae jane se sambandhit reporte samay samay praapt hoti rahati hai
 He said that according to the constitution of India, public order and police are the subjects of the state, so prevention and detection of crimes, investigation and registration is mainly a matter of state governments and union administrations
 unhone kaha ki dharmaataran rokane ke liye koi kanoon banane kaa prastaav nahin he
 As Prime Minister Manmohan Singh and his Pakistani counterpart Nawaz Sharif are expected to hold talks in New York later this month, India has said that an amicable atmosphere is needed for the meeting
 pakistan ne bharat ko is bare main soochna di he ki usne kaaphi samay se lambit mumbai hamale kii sunwaayee ke liye ek nayaa abhiyojak namit kiya he or ahm bhartiya gavaahon se jirah ke liye 23 sitambar ko ek nyaayik ayog vahaan bhejega, jisase jaanch main thos pragati ke liye kuch had tak nai dilli kii maang puri hogi
 Foreign Minister Salman Khurshid said that the Pakistani Prime Minister's Foreign Affairs Adviser Sartaj Aziz informed him of the development during an informal conversation in the capital of Kyrgyzstan on Thursday night
 ajij ne kaha ki khurshid ke saath unki baithak thik rahi or neuyork main is maheene ke aakhir main sanyukt raashtra mahasabha se itar donon deshon ke pradhanmantriyon ke bich vaarta ko protsaahit karne ke liye kootnithik str par prayaas jari rahenge
 Khurshid and Aziz are here to attend the Shanghai Cooperation Organization (SCO) conference
 ajij ke saath ratribhoj main shariq hue khurshid ne kaha, hamen ummid he or aashaa karte hai ki abhiyojak jald niyukt honge
 The evidence to be collected by the judicial commission will be made available to the Pakistani court
 purv abhiyojak kii hatya kar di gai thi
 He told that Aziz told him that the judicial commission would visit India on 23 September
 tippaniyan "we welcome this and we welcome the appointment of prosecutor," he told reporters
 khurshid ne kaha, or ham sachmuch main, eemaandaaree se yah aashaa karte hai ki ab chijen teji se aage badhengi or ham adaalat kii kaarywahi ke jariye dekhenge ki kuch thos chijen ho rahi hai
 The Foreign Minister said that he made Aziz aware that a cordial atmosphere would be needed for a possible meeting between the Prime Ministers of the two countries
 unhone kaha pradhanmantri manmohan singh ne bhi baar-baar yah rukh jaahir kiya he
 Khurshid said, "we told Aziz that there should be a cordial atmosphere in view of people's desire for positive dialogue
" jab kabhi ucch stareey vaarta ho, maahaul acha ho
 Stressing the need for peace along the indo-pak border, he said that the ceasefire along the Line of Control must be respected
 unhone kaha, yah bhi maahaul kaa hissaa he
 If there will be no peace on the border and on the Line of Control, the efforts will be in vain
 pakistan ne bharat ko is bare main soochna di he ki usne kaaphi samay se lambit mumbai hamale kii sunwaayee ke liye ek nayaa abhiyojak namit kiya he or ahm bhartiya gavaahon se jirah ke liye 23 sitambar ko ek nyaayik ayog vahaan bhejega, jisase jaanch main thos pragati ke liye kuch had tak nai dilli kii maang puri hogi

 unhone kaha, yah bhi maahaul kaa hissaa he
 If there will be no peace on the border and on the Line of Control, the efforts will be in vain
 videshmantri salmaan khurshid ne kaha ki pakistani pradhanmantri ke videsh maamalon ke salaahkaar sartaaj ajij ne unhen guuruuvaar kii raat kirgistan kii rajdhani main ek anaupchaarik baatcheet ke dauraan is ghatnakram kii jaankaree di
 Aziz said he had a good meeting with Khurshid and that diplomatic efforts would continue in New York later this month to encourage dialogue between the Prime Ministers of the two countries beyond the UN General Assembly
 khurshid or ajij shanghai sahyog sanghathan (essio) sammelan main shaamil hone ke liye yahaan aae hue hai
 Khurshid, who attended the dinner with Aziz, said, "we hope and hope that prosecutors will be appointed soon
" nyaayik ayog dwaara ekatra kiye jane vaale saboot pakistani adaalat ko uplabdh karaae jaaenge
 The former prosecutor was murdered
 unhone bataaya ki ajij ne unase kaha ki nyaayik ayog 23 sitambar ko bharat kii yatra par jayega
 The comments unhone samvaadadaataaon se kaha, ham iskaa swaagat karte hai or ham abhiyojak kii niyukti kaa swaagat karte hai
 Khurshid said, and we truly, sincerely hope that things will move fast now and we will see through the court proceedings that some concrete things are happening
 videshmantri ne bataaya ki unhone ajij ko is baat se avgat karaayaa ki donon deshon ke pradhanmantriyon ke bich sambhavit baithak ke liye ek sauhardpurn maahaul kii jarurat hogi
 He said that Prime Minister Manmohan Singh has also repeatedly expressed this stance
 khurshid ne kaha, hamane ajij se kaha ki sakaaratmak vaarta kii logon kii ichha ke maddenjar ek sauhardpurn maahaul hona chahie
 Whenever there is a high level of dialogue, the atmosphere is good
 unhone bharat-paak seemaa par shanti kii jarurat par jor dete hue kaha ki niyantran rekha par sangharsh viraam kaa sammaan avashya kiya janaa chahie
 He said, this is also part of the atmosphere
 yadi seemaa par or niyantran rekha par kisi tarah kii shanti nahin hogi, to koshishen bekaar ho jaaengi

 duusari ore bhrashtachar or kaale dhan kii chunauti desh ke saamne bani hui he

 bhrashtachar se arjeet cash kaa kaarobaar mahangaai par bada asar paidaa karata he

 eemaandaar vyakti ke liye kuch bhi khareednaa, ek madhyam varg ke vyakti ke liye ghar khareednaa ho, uske paas kala dhan nahin he to musiibat ho jaati he
 Due to this business of cash, there is a lot of artificial increase, artificial increase in the value of many services and goods like house, land, higher education and medicine
